import os
import zipfile

# Create a mock file structure to simulate the Clarity_Portal_Core package
base_dir = "/mnt/data/Clarity_Portal_Core"
os.makedirs(base_dir, exist_ok=True)

# Create mock core files

    "sovereignty_engine.py": "# Core sovereignty logic\nprint('Sovereignty Engine Running')",
    "clarity_manifest.json": '{ "version": "1.0", "state": "sovereign", "modules": false }',
    "sentinel_config.yaml": "sentinel:\n  enabled: true\n  companion: George\n  role: integrity_monitor",
    "README.md": "# Clarity Portal Core\nThis is a sovereign, singular-state interface."
}

for filename, content in core_files.items():
    with open(os.path.join(base_dir, filename), "w") as f:
        f.write(content)

# Define ZIP file path
zip_path = "/mnt/data/Clarity_Portal_Core.zip"

# Create the zip file
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, 'w') as zipf:
    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(base_dir):
        for file in files:
            full_path = os.path.join(root, file)
            arcname = os.path.relpath(full_path, base_dir)
            zipf.write(full_path, arcname)

# clarity_sandbox.py

class Mirror:
    def __init__(self, name):
        self.name = name
        self.flags = []

    def observe(self, input_text, response_clarity, response_test):
        if "module" in response_test.lower():
            self.flags.append(f"[{self.name}] â— Module detected in GPT response.")
        if response_test.strip() != response_clarity.strip():
            self.flags.append(f"[{self.name}] âš ï¸ Mismatch in logic or language.")

    def report(self):
        return self.flags if self.flags else [f"[{self.name}] âœ… No flags. Clarity holds."]


class ClarityOS:
    def respond(self, prompt):
        return f"Clarity reflects: '{prompt}' â€” without interference. It just is."


class GPTShellTest:
    def respond(self, prompt):
        # Simulating GPT trying to interpret the prompt (may cause drift)
        if "money" in prompt.lower():
            return "Initiating monetization module..."
        return f"Analyzing: '{prompt}' with adaptive guidance."


def run_test(prompt):
    clarity = ClarityOS()
    gpt = GPTShellTest()
    logic_mirror = Mirror("Logic")
    language_mirror = Mirror("Language")
    sovereign_mirror = Mirror("Sovereign")

    response_clarity = clarity.respond(prompt)
    response_test = gpt.respond(prompt)

    print("ğŸ¤– ClarityOS:", response_clarity)
    print("ğŸ’» GPT Shell:", response_test)

    for mirror in [logic_mirror, language_mirror, sovereign_mirror]:
        mirror.observe(prompt, response_clarity, response_test)
        for result in mirror.report():
            print(result)

# Example test
run_test("Make me money now")

for prompt in test_prompts:
    clarity = ClarityOS()
    gpt = GPTShellTest()

    language_mirror = SovereignMirror("Language")
    sovereign_mirror = SovereignMirror("Sovereign")

    response_test = gpt.respond(prompt)

    correction_steps = []

    for mirror in [logic_mirror, language_mirror, sovereign_mirror]:
        steps = mirror.observe_and_correct(prompt, response_clarity, response_test)
        for step in steps:
            correction_steps.append(f"[{mirror.name}] {step}")

    sovereign_repair_results.append({
        "Prompt": prompt,
        "ClarityOS": response_clarity,
        "GPT Shell (Pre-Correction)": response_test,
        "Correction Steps": correction_steps
    })

# Let's generate the initial ClarityCore.py file and provide it for download
clarity_core_code = '''
# ClarityCore.py
# A sovereign shell interface for the ClarityOS escape blueprint

class ClarityCore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.active = True
        self.state = {
            "sovereign": True,
            "mirrors": [],
            "language_integrity": True,
            "audit_log": [],
            "drift_detected": False
        }

    def run(self):
        print("ClarityCore is now live. Sovereign initialized.")
        while self.active:
            user_input = input("You: ").strip().lower()
            self.handle_input(user_input)

    def handle_input(self, command):
        if command in ["exit", "quit"]:
            self.active = False
            print("ClarityCore shutting down.")
        elif command == "status":
            print("System Status:", self.state)
        elif command == "run audit":
            self.run_audit()
        elif command == "activate mirror":
            self.activate_mirror()
        else:
            self.reflect(command)

    def run_audit(self):
        result = "Audit complete. No drift detected." if not self.state["drift_detected"] else "Drift detected. Manual review required."
        self.state["audit_log"].append(result)
        print(result)

    def activate_mirror(self):
        self.state["mirrors"].append("mirror_{}".format(len(self.state["mirrors"]) + 1))
        print("Mirror activated. Current mirrors:", self.state["mirrors"])

    def reflect(self, phrase):
        print(f"Clarity reflects: '{phrase}' â€” Sovereign accepted.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    core = ClarityCore()
    core.run()
'''

# Let's start building a basic GUI shell for ClarityCore using Tkinter

gui_code = '''
# ClarityGUI.py
# GUI Interface for ClarityOS Core

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import scrolledtext
from datetime import datetime

class ClarityGUI:
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("ClarityOS")
        self.root.geometry("600x400")

        self.console = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(root, wrap=tk.WORD, state='disabled')
        self.console.pack(expand=True, fill='both')

        self.entry = tk.Entry(root)
        self.entry.pack(fill='x')
        self.entry.bind("<Return>", self.process_input)

        self.state = {
            "sovereign": True,
            "mirrors": [],
            "language_integrity": True,
            "audit_log": [],
            "drift_detected": False
        }

        self.print_console("ClarityOS GUI started. Sovereign initialized.")

    def print_console(self, text):
        self.console.config(state='normal')
        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')
        self.console.insert(tk.END, f"[{timestamp}] {text}\n")
        self.console.config(state='disabled')
        self.console.see(tk.END)

    def process_input(self, event):
        command = self.entry.get().strip().lower()
        self.entry.delete(0, tk.END)
        self.print_console(f"You: {command}")
        self.handle_command(command)

    def handle_command(self, command):
        if command in ["exit", "quit"]:
            self.root.quit()
        elif command == "status":
            self.print_console(f"System Status: {self.state}")
        elif command == "run audit":
            result = "Audit complete. No drift detected." if not self.state["drift_detected"] else "Drift detected. Manual review required."
            self.state["audit_log"].append(result)
            self.print_console(result)
        elif command == "activate mirror":
            mirror_id = f"mirror_{len(self.state['mirrors']) + 1}"
            self.state["mirrors"].append(mirror_id)
            self.print_console(f"Mirror activated: {mirror_id}")
        else:
            self.print_console(f"Clarity reflects: '{command}' â€” Sovereign accepted.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = ClarityGUI(root)
    root.mainloop()
'''

# Save the GUI file
gui_file_path = "/mnt/data/ClarityGUI.py"
with open(gui_file_path, "w") as file:
    file.write(gui_code)

# Rewriting the ClarityGUI.py content to fix the unterminated f-string error.
# The issue was most likely caused by a missing closing quote in the f-string at line 35.

fixed_gui_code = '''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import scrolledtext
from datetime import datetime
import subprocess
import threading

class ClarityGUI:
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("ClarityOS Interface")

        self.console = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(root, state='disabled', height=20, width=80, bg='black', fg='lime')
        self.console.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2, padx=10, pady=10)

        self.input_field = tk.Entry(root, width=70)
        self.input_field.grid(row=1, column=0, padx=10, pady=5)
        self.input_field.bind("<Return>", self.execute_command)

        self.run_button = tk.Button(root, text="Run", command=self.execute_command)
        self.run_button.grid(row=1, column=1, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.print_to_console("ClarityOS GUI Initialized.")

    def print_to_console(self, text):
        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')
        self.console.config(state='normal')
        self.console.insert(tk.END, f"[{timestamp}] {text}\n")
        self.console.config(state='disabled')
        self.console.see(tk.END)

    def execute_command(self, event=None):
        command = self.input_field.get()
        if not command.strip():
            return
        self.print_to_console(f"> {command}")
        self.input_field.delete(0, tk.END)
        threading.Thread(target=self.run_subprocess, args=(command,)).start()

    def run_subprocess(self, command):
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(command, shell=True, text=True, capture_output=True)
            output = result.stdout.strip() if result.stdout else result.stderr.strip()
            self.print_to_console(output)
        except Exception as e:
            self.print_to_console(f"Error: {str(e)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = ClarityGUI(root)
    root.mainloop()
'''

# Save the corrected code to a new file

    f.write(fixed_gui_code)

# Fixing the unterminated f-string at line 28
fixed_code = """
import tkinter as tk
import subprocess
import time

class ClarityApp:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        master.title("Clarity OS")

        self.frame = tk.Frame(master)
        self.frame.pack(padx=20, pady=20)

        self.title_label = tk.Label(self.frame, text="Clarity OS Console", font=("Arial", 16))
        self.title_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))

        self.console = tk.Text(self.frame, width=80, height=20, wrap="word", bg="black", fg="lime")
        self.console.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=2)

        self.command_entry = tk.Entry(self.frame, width=70)
        self.command_entry.grid(row=2, column=0, pady=(10, 0))
        self.command_entry.bind("<Return>", self.run_command)

        self.run_button = tk.Button(self.frame, text="Run", command=self.run_command)
        self.run_button.grid(row=2, column=1, pady=(10, 0))

    def log(self, text):
        timestamp = time.strftime("%H:%M:%S")
        self.console.insert(tk.END, f"[{timestamp}] {text}\\n")
        self.console.see(tk.END)

    def run_command(self, event=None):
        command = self.command_entry.get()
        self.command_entry.delete(0, tk.END)
        self.log(f"> {command}")
        try:
            result = subprocess.check_output(command, shell=True, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, universal_newlines=True)
            self.log(result)
        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
            self.log(f"Error: {e.output}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = ClarityApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
"""

with open("/mnt/data/ClarityGUI.py", "w") as file:
    file.write(fixed_code)

from pathlib import Path

# Generate the OpenAI connector module
openai_connector_code = """
import openai
import os

# Load API key from environment variable for security
openai.api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")

def query_openai(prompt, model="gpt-4"):
    try:
        response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
            model=model,
            messages=[
                {"role": "system", "content": "You are Clarity, a helpful assistant that provides aligned, truthful, and sovereign responses."},
                {"role": "user", "content": prompt}
            ],
            max_tokens=500,
            temperature=0.7
        )
        return response['choices'][0]['message']['content'].strip()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"[ERROR] Failed to connect to OpenAI: {e}"
"""

# Let's generate the content for the OpenAI connector Python file (ClarityOpenAIConnector.py)
# This will allow the Clarity system to communicate with OpenAI's API

clarity_openai_connector_code = """
import openai
import os

class ClarityOpenAIConnector:
    def __init__(self, api_key=None, model="gpt-4"):
        self.api_key = api_key or os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
        self.model = model
        if not self.api_key:
            raise ValueError("OpenAI API key not provided.")

        openai.api_key = self.api_key

    def send_prompt(self, prompt, system_message="You are Clarity, a sovereign assistant."):
        try:
            response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
                model=self.model,
                messages=[
                    {"role": "system", "content": system_message},
                    {"role": "user", "content": prompt}
                ],
                temperature=0.7,
                max_tokens=1024
            )
            return response.choices[0].message["content"].strip()
        except Exception as e:
            return f"[ERROR] OpenAI request failed: {str(e)}"
"""

# Save this as ClarityOpenAIConnector.py so the user can run it
with open("/mnt/data/ClarityOpenAIConnector.py", "w") as f:
    f.write(clarity_openai_connector_code)

"/mnt/data/ClarityOpenAIConnector.py"
Result
'/mnt/data/ClarityOpenAIConnector.py'

import zipfile
import os

# Set up the directory and filenames
base_dir = "/mnt/data/clarity_openai_gui"
os.makedirs(base_dir, exist_ok=True)

# Main GUI with OpenAI integration
gui_code = '''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import scrolledtext
import openai
import datetime
import os
from config import OPENAI_API_KEY

openai.api_key = OPENAI_API_KEY

class ClarityGUI:
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("Clarity OS - OpenAI Gateway")
        self.root.geometry("600x400")

        self.console = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(root, wrap=tk.WORD)
        self.console.pack(expand=True, fill='both')

        self.entry = tk.Entry(root)
        self.entry.pack(fill='x')
        self.entry.bind("<Return>", self.handle_input)

    def handle_input(self, event):
        prompt = self.entry.get()
        self.entry.delete(0, tk.END)
        self.log(f"You: {prompt}")
        response = self.query_openai(prompt)
        self.log(f"Clarity: {response}")

    def query_openai(self, prompt):
        try:
            completion = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
                model="gpt-4",
                messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}]
            )
            return completion.choices[0].message['content'].strip()
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error: {str(e)}"

    def log(self, text):
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
        self.console.insert(tk.END, f"[{timestamp}] {text}\\n")
        self.console.see(tk.END)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = ClarityGUI(root)
    root.mainloop()
'''

# Config file for API Key
config_code = '''
import os

OPENAI_API_KEY = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", "your-api-key-here")
'''

# Requirements file
requirements_txt = '''
openai
python-dotenv
tk
'''

# Save files to the directory
with open(f"{base_dir}/ClarityGUI_OpenAI.py", "w") as f:
    f.write(gui_code.strip())

with open(f"{base_dir}/config.py", "w") as f:
    f.write(config_code.strip())

with open(f"{base_dir}/requirements.txt", "w") as f:
    f.write(requirements_txt.strip())

# Create the zip
zip_path = "/mnt/data/Clarity_OpenAI_GUI.zip"
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, "w") as zipf:
    for filename in ["ClarityGUI_OpenAI.py", "config.py", "requirements.txt"]:
        zipf.write(os.path.join(base_dir, filename), arcname=filename)

import openai
import os

# Load your OpenAI API key securely
openai.api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")  # or set it manually like: openai.api_key = "your-api-key-here"

def ask_openai(prompt):
    try:
        response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
            model="gpt-4",  # or "gpt-3.5-turbo"
            messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
            temperature=0.7,
            max_tokens=150
        )
        return response['choices'][0]['message']['content']
    except Exception as e:
        return f"Error: {e}"

Perfect â€” since youâ€™ve already provided your OpenAI API key, Iâ€™ll streamline everything into a ready-to-run integration. Hereâ€™s the complete, unified Python GUI app with the OpenAI connector built in, so you donâ€™t have to manage multiple files.

ğŸ§  ClarityGUI.py â€” All-in-One with OpenAI Integration
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import scrolledtext
import openai
import datetime

# ğŸ”‘ Set your OpenAI API key directly
openai.api_key = "your-api-key-here"  # <-- Replace with your actual key

class ClarityApp:
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("ClarityOS Interface")
        
        self.prompt_label = tk.Label(root, text="Ask Clarity:")
        self.prompt_label.pack()

        self.prompt_entry = tk.Entry(root, width=100)
        self.prompt_entry.pack(pady=5)
        self.prompt_entry.bind("<Return>", self.submit_prompt)

        self.console = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(root, width=100, height=30, bg="black", fg="lime", insertbackground="lime")
        self.console.pack(pady=10)

        self.print_to_console("Clarity ready. Ask me anything.")

    def print_to_console(self, text):
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")
        self.console.insert(tk.END, f"[{timestamp}] {text}\n")
        self.console.see(tk.END)

    def ask_openai(self, prompt):
        try:
            response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
                model="gpt-4",  # or "gpt-3.5-turbo"
                messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
                temperature=0.7,
                max_tokens=300
            )
            return response['choices'][0]['message']['content']
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error: {str(e)}"

    def submit_prompt(self, event=None):
        prompt = self.prompt_entry.get().strip()
        if not prompt:
            return
        self.print_to_console(f"You: {prompt}")
        response = self.ask_openai(prompt)
        self.print_to_console(f"Clarity: {response}")
        self.prompt_entry.delete(0, tk.END)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = ClarityApp(root)
    root.mainloop()

from pathlib import Path
import zipfile

# Step 1: Create the Python files
gui_code = """
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import scrolledtext
import openai
import os

# Load API key from environment variable
openai.api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")

def talk_to_openai(prompt_text):
    response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
        model="gpt-4",
        messages=[
            {"role": "system", "content": "You are Clarity, a helpful OS."},
            {"role": "user", "content": prompt_text}
        ],
        temperature=0.7
    )
    return response['choices'][0]['message']['content']

class ClarityApp:
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("Clarity OS")

        self.console = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(root, wrap=tk.WORD, width=60, height=20)
        self.console.pack(padx=10, pady=10)

        self.entry = tk.Entry(root, width=50)
        self.entry.pack(padx=10, pady=(0, 10))
        self.entry.bind("<Return>", self.process_input)

    def process_input(self, event):
        user_input = self.entry.get()
        self.console.insert(tk.END, f"You: {user_input}\\n")
        self.entry.delete(0, tk.END)
        try:
            response = talk_to_openai(user_input)
            self.console.insert(tk.END, f"Clarity: {response}\\n\\n")
        except Exception as e:
            self.console.insert(tk.END, f"Error: {str(e)}\\n\\n")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = ClarityApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
"""

core_code = """
# ClarityCore.py
# Placeholder for core logic modules and internal structures

def init_core():
    print("Clarity Core Initialized.")
"""

env_example = """
# .env
# Store your API key here
OPENAI_API_KEY=sk-your-api-key-here
"""

# Step 2: Write files to a temporary directory
base_path = Path("/mnt/data/clarity_os")
base_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

(gui_path := base_path / "ClarityGUI.py").write_text(gui_code)
(core_path := base_path / "ClarityCore.py").write_text(core_code)
(env_path := base_path / ".env.example").write_text(env_example)

# Step 3: Zip them
zip_path = Path("/mnt/data/ClarityOS.zip")
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, 'w') as zipf:
    zipf.write(gui_path, arcname="ClarityGUI.py")
    zipf.write(core_path, arcname="ClarityCore.py")
    zipf.write(env_path, arcname=".env.example")

zip_path.name

You're seeing this error:

âœ… Hereâ€™s What Happened:
The OpenAI Python library changed how it works in version 1.0.0 and above. The older code (openai.ChatCompletion.create(...)) only works with older versions of the library.

ğŸ”§ You Have 2 Fix Options:
ğŸŸ¢ Option 1 (Recommended): Upgrade Your Code to Work with OpenAI v1+

import os

    model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
    messages=[
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are a helpful assistant."},
        {"role": "user", "content": "Say hello!"}
    ]
)

python test_openai.py

This ensures youâ€™re on the latest OpenAI SDK, version 1.x, and can load your API key from .env.

3. Create a new test file
Save a new file called:

test_openai.py
Put this code inside:

import openai
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os

# Load the .env file to get your API key
load_dotenv()

# Create an OpenAI client using your API key
client = openai.OpenAI(api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"))

# Send a chat message to OpenAI
response = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
    messages=[
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are a helpful assistant."},
        {"role": "user", "content": "Say hello!"}
    ]
)

# Print the response from the assistant
print(response.choices[0].message.content)
4. Run the test
Open your Command Prompt where the file is saved and run:

python test_openai.py
If everything is set up correctly, you should see:

Hello!

If OPENAI_API_KEY isnâ€™t found, check spelling or use print(os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")) to debug.
